# <a name="com-error-codes-tpm-pla-fve"></a><span data-ttu-id="2947b-104">COM 錯誤碼 (TPM、PLA、FVE) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-104">COM Error Codes (TPM, PLA, FVE)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2947b-105">下表提供以 COM 為基礎的 Api 所使用的錯誤碼清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-105">The following table provides a list of error codes used by COM-based APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2947b-106">如果您在安裝或執行的應用程式遇到困難，請洽詢客戶對顯示錯誤訊息之軟體的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-106">If you are experiencing difficulty with an application you are installing or running, contact customer support for the software that is displaying the error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2947b-107">若要取得 Microsoft 產品的支援，請移至 [https://support.microsoft.com](https://support.microsoft.com) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-107">To obtain support for a Microsoft product, go to [https://support.microsoft.com](https://support.microsoft.com).</span></span>

| <span id="FVE_E_DEVICELOCKOUT_COUNTER_MISMATCH"></span><span id="fve_e_devicelockout_counter_mismatch"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2947b-1323"><dt>**FVE \_E \_ DEVICELOCKOUT \_ 計數器 \_ 不符**</dt> <dt>0x803100CE</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-1323"><dt>**FVE\_E\_DEVICELOCKOUT\_COUNTER\_MISMATCH**</dt> <dt>0x803100CE</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                | <span data-ttu-id="2947b-1324">因為計數器不符，所以裝置鎖定狀態驗證失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-1324">Device Lockout state validation failed due to counter mismatch.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span id="FVE_E_BUFFER_TOO_LARGE"></span><span id="fve_e_buffer_too_large"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2947b-1325"><dt>**FVE \_E \_ 緩衝區 \_ 太 \_ 大**</dt> <dt>0x803100CF</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-1325"><dt>**FVE\_E\_BUFFER\_TOO\_LARGE**</dt> <dt>0x803100CF</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                                                                          | <span data-ttu-id="2947b-1326">輸入緩衝區太大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2947b-1326">The input buffer is too large.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
